kushal@fedora:~/src/dotnet/MyDesktopApplication$ time bash fix-app-update.sh 
==============================================
  Fixing App Update Issues - All Platforms
==============================================

[STEP] 1/4 - Updating Directory.Build.props for centralized versioning...
  ✓ Directory.Build.props updated
[STEP] 2/4 - Updating Android project for dynamic versioning...
  ✓ Android csproj updated with dynamic versioning
[STEP] 3/4 - Updating Desktop project for consistent versioning...
  ✓ Desktop csproj updated
[STEP] 4/4 - Updating GitHub Actions workflow...
  ✓ GitHub Actions workflow updated

==============================================
  Fix Complete!
==============================================

Changes made:
  • Directory.Build.props: Centralized versioning with BuildNumber property
  • Android .csproj: Dynamic ApplicationVersion based on BuildNumber
  • Desktop .csproj: Consistent versioning
  • GitHub Actions: Passes BuildNumber=${{ github.run_number }} to all builds

How versioning now works:

  Local development:
    - BuildNumber defaults to 0
    - Android versionCode = 1, versionName = 1.0.0-local
    - Desktop AssemblyVersion = 1.0.0.0

  CI builds (GitHub Actions):
    - BuildNumber = github.run_number (42, 43, 44, ...)
    - Android versionCode = 42, versionName = 1.0.42
    - Desktop AssemblyVersion = 1.0.42.0
    - Release tag = v1.0.42

Why this fixes Android updates:
  Android requires versionCode to strictly increase for updates.
  github.run_number automatically increments with every push,
  so each APK has a higher versionCode than the previous one.
  Obtainium and manual sideloading will recognize these as updates.

To apply:
  git add -A
  git commit -m 'Fix app update versioning for all platforms'
  git push

After the next push, the APK will have:
  - versionCode: (next run number)
  - versionName: 1.0.(next run number)

And Android will install it as an update, no uninstall needed!
